## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / classical mechanics (nonlinear oscillators)
**Analysis**: The target dv_dt is acceleration, with state variables x (position) and v (velocity), indicating a second-order ODE x'' = f(x,v,t) typical of damped/driven nonlinear harmonic oscillators (e.g., Duffing, van der Pol, pendulum). Relationships usually combine a restoring term in x, damping in v, and possibly time-periodic forcing or parametric modulation in t.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear harmonic oscillator (undamped): dv_dt = -c0 * x (restoring force proportional to displacement)
- Linear viscous damping: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v (mass-normalized spring + dashpot)
- Time-dependent stiffness (parametric oscillator): dv_dt = -(c0 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) * x - c3 * v (Mathieu-type / parametrically excited systems)
- Sinusoidal external forcing: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (driven damped oscillator)
- Duffing oscillator (cubic stiffness): dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * x**3 - c2 * v (hardening/softening spring nonlinearity)
- Higher-order restoring nonlinearity: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * x**3 - c2 * x**5 - c3 * v (strongly nonlinear spring/potential expansion)
- Pendulum restoring force: dv_dt = -c0 * sin(c1 * x) - c2 * v (large-angle nonlinear oscillator with damping)
- Quadratic/velocity-squared drag: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v * Abs(v) (aerodynamic-like damping in oscillation)
- Rayleigh-type nonlinear damping: dv_dt = -c0 * x - (c1 - c2 * v**2) * v (amplitude-dependent damping; can yield self-excitation)
- van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = -c0 * x + c1 * (1 - c2 * x**2) * v (negative damping at small |x|, positive at large |x|; limit cycles)
- State-coupled stiffness/damping: dv_dt = -(c0 + c1 * x**2) * x - (c2 + c3 * x**2) * v (amplitude-dependent frequency and dissipation)
- Conservative potential-gradient form (polynomial potential): dv_dt = -(c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5) (energy-conserving oscillator with nonlinear potential)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope тЖТ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects тЖТ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay тЖТ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior тЖТ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects тЖТ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Purely conservative oscillators often have dv_dt depending only on x (no v term); adding v terms typically models dissipation or active driving.
- Restoring forces for symmetric potentials are typically odd in x (e.g., x, x**3, sin(c*x)); even powers in the force often indicate asymmetry or bias.
- Hardening vs softening springs correspond to the sign of the cubic stiffness term in dv_dt ~ -c*x - c'*x**3, producing amplitude-dependent frequency shifts.
- Viscous damping appears as a linear odd-in-v term (-c*v); quadratic drag appears as -c*v*Abs(v), dominating at high speeds.
- Self-excited/limit-cycle behavior is suggested by тАЬnegative damping at small amplitude, positive at large amplitudeтАЭ terms like (1 - c*x**2)*v or (c - v**2)*v.
- External periodic forcing typically enters additively as sin(c*t) or cos(c*t), producing resonance/entrainment phenomena.
- Parametric excitation typically multiplies x via time-periodic coefficients (c0 + c1*cos(c2*t)) * x, associated with Mathieu-type instabilities.
- Coupling terms such as x**2*v indicate amplitude-dependent dissipation (damping increases with displacement), common in nonlinear structural vibrations.
- If dv_dt contains no explicit t, the system is autonomous; explicit t terms indicate non-autonomous forcing/modulation and can yield quasiperiodic/chaotic responses.

The GT has these basis function components:
1. A term linear in `x` (coefficient of `x`)
2. A term `x * |v|^(1/3)` 
3. A term `x * exp(-|x|)`
4. A term `sin(t)`

This is a very specific combination. Let me check each candidate:

**Key observations about GT structure:**
- Contains `x * |v|^(1/3)` тАФ needs a `v`-dependent term multiplied by `x`
- Contains `x * exp(-|x|)` тАФ needs an exponential of `|x|` multiplied by `x`
- Contains `sin(t)` тАФ sinusoidal in `t`
- Contains linear `x` term

Let me go through candidates systematically:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2 + c3*t) + c4*log(c5*x + 1) + c6*x**c7 + c8*x**c9`
- No `v` dependence, no `exp(-|x|)` term. Has `log` and power terms instead. Cannot match.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2*t + c3) + c4*x**c5 + c6*x**c7 + c8*cos(t)`
- No `v` dependence, no `exp(-|x|)`. Cannot match.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `c0*x + c1*x**3 + c2*sin(c3 + c4*t) + c5*x**c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)`
- No `v` dependence, has `exp(c8*t)` not `x*exp(-|x|)`. Cannot match.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2 + c3*t) + c4*sin(c5*t + c6) + c7*x**c8`
- No `v` dependence, no `exp(-|x|)`. Two sin terms can combine but still missing key terms.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2 + c3*t) + c4 + c5*x**c6 + c7*v**c8*x`
- Has `v**c8 * x` тАФ with c8=1/3, this gives `v^(1/3)*x`. But this is `v^(1/3)`, not `|v|^(1/3)`. Since `v` takes both signs, `v^(1/3)` is defined but differs from `|v|^(1/3)` (for negative v, `v^(1/3)` is negative while `|v|^(1/3)` is positive). Also has `x**c6` but needs `x*exp(-|x|)`. Cannot match.
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2*t + c3) + c4*x**c5 + c6*cos(c7*t)`
- No `v` dependence, no `exp(-|x|)`. Cannot match.
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 7:** `c0*tanh(c1*x + c2) + c3*x + c4*sin(c5*t + c6) + c7*v*(c8 + x)**c9`
- Has `v*(c8+x)^c9` тАФ this is linear in `v`, not `|v|^(1/3)*x`. Also `tanh` тЙа `x*exp(-|x|)`. Cannot match.
Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 8:** `c0*tanh(c1*x + c2) + c3*x + c4*sin(c5*t + c6)`
- No `v` dependence, `tanh` тЙа `x*exp(-|x|)`. Cannot match.
Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 9:** `c0*tanh(c1*x + c2) + c3*sin(c4*t + c5) + c6*x + c7`
- Same issues as 8.
Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 10:** `c0*tanh(c1*x) + c2*sin(c3*t + c4) + c5*x + c6`
- No `v` dependence, `tanh` тЙа `x*exp(-|x|)`.
Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 11:** `c0*tanh(c1*x + c2) + c3*x + c4*log(c5*x + 1) + c6*sin(c7*t + c8)`
- No `v` dependence. Cannot match.
Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 12:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2*t + c3) + c4*log(c5*t + 1) + c6*x**c7 + c8*cos(c9*t)`
- No `v` dependence, has `log(t)` term. Cannot match.
Candidate 12 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 13:** `c0*tanh(c1*x + c2) + c3*sin(c4*v + c5) + c6*x + c7*sin(c8*t + c9)`
- Has `sin(c4*v + c5)` тАФ sinusoidal in `v`, not `|v|^(1/3)*x`. Cannot match.
Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 14:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2 + c3*t) + c4*sin(c5*x + c6) + c7*x**c8`
- No `v` dependence. `sin(x)` тЙа `x*exp(-|x|)`. Cannot match.
Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 15:** `c0*x + c1*x**3 + c2*sin(c3*x + c4) + c5*sin(c6 + c7*t) + c8`
- No `v` dependence. Cannot match.
Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 16:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2 + c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*x**c7`
- No `v` dependence. Cannot match.
Candidate 16 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidates 17-28, 30-35, 37-48:** Let me scan for any that have both `v` dependence AND `exp(-|x|)` or equivalent structure.

Looking through all remaining candidates:
- **Candidate 29:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2 + c3*t) + c4 + c5*x**c6 + c7*x*(c8 + v)**c9`
  Has `x*(c8+v)^c9`. With c9=1/3, this gives `x*(c8+v)^(1/3)`. This is NOT `x*|v|^(1/3)` unless c8=0, but even then `(v)^(1/3) тЙа |v|^(1/3)` for negative v. Also missing `x*exp(-|x|)`.
Candidate 29 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 36:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2 + c3*t) + c4 + c5*x**c6 + c7*(c8 + v)**c9`
- Has `(c8+v)^c9` but not multiplied by `x`. Missing `x*exp(-|x|)`.
Candidate 36 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 41:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2*t + c3) + c4*v/(c5*t + c6) + c7/(c5*t + c6) + tanh(c8*x + c9)`
- Has `v` but in wrong form. Cannot match.
Candidate 41 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 44:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2*t + c3) + c4*v*(c5 + t)**c6 + tanh(c7*x + c8)`
- Has `v*(c5+t)^c6` тАФ wrong structure.
Candidate 44 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 49:** `c0*tanh(c1*x) + c2*sin(c3*t + c4) + c5*sin(c6*t + c7) + c8*t*x`
- Has `t*x` term, no proper `v` dependence.
Candidate 49 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 50:** `c0*tanh(c1*x) + c2*sin(c3*t + c4) + c5*sin(c6*t + c7)`
- No `v` dependence.
Candidate 50 verdict: [NO MATCH]
